Expectation\n```\n\n4. **Consequences:** Verify state after actions\n```go\n// /workspace/test/e2e/fixture/app/consequences.go\ntype Consequences struct {\n    // ... fields\n}\n\nfunc (c *Consequences) And(a func(app *Application)) *Consequences\nfunc (c *Consequences) Expect(expectations ...Expectation) *Consequences\nfunc (c *Consequences) Then() *Consequences\n```\n\n---\n\n### 6. E2E TEST STRUCTURE (GWT Pattern)\n\nThe E2E tests use a sophisticated **Given-When-Then** pattern with fluent API:\n\n**Architecture:**\n```\nfixture.go          - Main fixture initialization and setup\n├── fixture/fixture.go (36KB) - E2E test infrastructure\n├── fixture/cmd.go       - Command execution\n├── fixture/util.go      - Utilities\n├── fixture/tmpl.go      - Template handling\n└── fixture/http.go      - HTTP utilities\n\nfixture/app/         - Application-specific fixtures\n├── context.go        - \"Given\" phase (test setup)\n├── actions.go        - \"When\" phase (test actions)\n├── expectation.go    - \"Then\" phase (assertions)\n└── consequences.go   - Result handling\n\nfixture/account/     - Account/user fixtures\nfixture/admin/       - Admin fixtures\nfixture/cluster/     - Cluster fixtures\nfixture/project/     - Project fixtures\nfixture/repos/       - Repository fixtures\nfixture/applicationsets/ - ApplicationSet fixtures\nfixture/notification/  - Notification fixtures\n```\n\n**Pattern Components:**\n\n1. **Context (Given Phase):** Setup test state\n```go\n// /workspace/test/e2e/fixture/app/context.go\ntype Context struct {\n    t *testing.T\n    path string\n    chart string\n    repoURLType fixture.RepoURLType\n    timeout int\n    name string\n    // ... more fields\n}\n\nfunc Given(t *testing.T, opts ...fixture.TestOption) *Context\nfunc GivenWithSameState(t *testing.T) *Context\n```\n\n2. **Actions (When Phase):** Perform operations\n```go\n// /workspace/test/e2e/fixture/app/actions.go\ntype Actions struct {\n    context *Context\n    lastOutput string\n    lastError error\n    ignoreErrors bool\n}\n\nfunc (a *Actions) CreateApp() *Actions\nfunc (a *Actions) Sync() *Actions\nfunc (a *Actions) WriteFile(fileName, fileContents string) *Actions\nfunc (a *Actions) PatchFile(file string, jsonPath string) *Actions\n```\n\n3. **Expectation (Then Phase):** Assert results\n```go\n// /workspace/test/e2e/fixture/app/expectation.go\ntype Expectation func(c *Consequences) (state state, message string)\n\nfunc OperationPhaseIs(expected OperationPhase) Expectation\nfunc SyncStatusIs(expected SyncStatusCode) Expectation\nfunc HealthIs(expected HealthStatus) Expectation\nfunc Condition(conditionType ApplicationConditionType, ...) Expectation\n```\n\n4. **Consequences:** Verify state after actions\n```go\n// /workspace/test/e2e/fixture/app/consequences.go\ntype Consequences struct {\n    // ... fields\n}\n\nfunc (c *Consequences) And(a func(app *Application)) *Consequences\nfunc (c *Consequences) Expect(expectations ...Expectation) *Consequences\nfunc (c *Consequences) Then() *Consequences\n```\n\n---\n\n### 6. Key Sync State Transitions\n\n```\nNormal Sync Flow (Healthy App):\n  OutOfSync → [user triggers sync] → OperationPending \n    → OperationRunning → OperationSucceeded \n    → Synced (after next refresh)\n\nAuto-Sync Flow:\n  OutOfSync → (app controller detects & auto-syncs)\n    → OperationPending → OperationRunning \n    → OperationSucceeded → Synced\n\nRetry Flow (Failed Sync):\n  OutOfSync → OperationRunning → OperationFailed \n    → (retry with backoff) → OperationRunning \n    → OperationSucceeded → Synced\n\nFailure States:\n  ComparisonError → status Unknown (can't determine state)\n  SyncError → OperationFailed (explicit failure)\n  InvalidSpec → OperationError (bad config)\n```\n\n### 11. CRD Type Definitions\n\n**Location:** `/workspace/pkg/apis/application/v1alpha1/types.go`\n\nThe Application CRD is defined with these key structures:\n\n```\nApplication CRD\n├── Spec (ApplicationSpec)\n│   ├── Source/Sources: ApplicationSource (git repo reference)\n│   ├── Destination: ApplicationDestination (target cluster/namespace)\n│   ├── Project: AppProject reference\n│   └── SyncPolicy: Controls automatic syncing\n├── Status (ApplicationStatus)\n│   ├── Sync: SyncStatus (Synced/OutOfSync/Unknown)\n│   ├── Health: HealthStatus (Healthy/Degraded/Unknown)\n│   ├── Resources: []ResourceStatus (managed resources)\n│   └── OperationState: Current operation status\n└── Operation: Requested operation (Sync, Rollback, etc.)\n```\n\n### 2. Controller Reconciliation Entry Points\n\n**Location:** `/workspace/controller/appcontroller.go`\n\nThe ApplicationController reconciles through two main queues:\n\n```\nappRefreshQueue (Status Reconciliation)\n  └─> processAppRefreshQueueItem()\n      └─> Runs status refresh periodically based on needRefreshAppStatus()\n\nappOperationQueue (Sync Operations)\n  └─> processAppOperationQueueItem()\n      └─> Processes user-requested sync operations\n```\n\n### 3. Main Reconciliation Loop - Status Refresh\n\n**Method:** `processAppRefreshQueueItem()` (line 1541 in appcontroller.go)\n\n```\nStatus Refresh Cycle:\n1. Check needRefreshAppStatus() - determines comparison level:\n   - ComparisonWithNothing (0): Just update resource tree\n   - CompareWithRecent (1): Compare with cached revision\n   - CompareWithLatest (2): Compare with latest in git\n   - CompareWithLatestForceResolve (3): Force re-resolve git ref\n\n2. refreshAppConditions() - validate application config\n\n3. CompareAppState() [State Manager]\n   ├─> GetRepoObjs() - Fetch target manifests from repo-server\n   ├─> liveStateCache.GetManagedLiveObjs() - Get live cluster state\n   ├─> sync.Reconcile() [gitops-engine] - Match live and target\n   └─> Calculate diff and sync status\n\n4. setAppManagedResources() - Update status.resources\n\n5. persistAppStatus() - Patch Application CR with new status\n```\n\n### 4. State Manager - CompareAppState Implementation\n\n**Location:** `/workspace/controller/state.go` (line 429)\n\n```\nCompareAppState Pipeline:\n\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│ 1. Load Comparison Settings                                      │\n│    - AppLabelKey, ResourceOverrides, ResourceFilters             │\n│    - Enable source types, Helm repos, credentials                │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n           ↓\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│ 2. Get Target Objects from Repo-Server                           │\n│    - GetRepoObjs() via gRPC to repo-server                       │\n│    - Supports: Helm, Kustomize, Directory, Plugin               │\n│    - Returns: Unstructured manifests + revision info             │\n│    - Caches manifests based on revision                          │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n           ↓\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│ 3. Get Live Objects from Cluster Cache                           │\n│    - liveStateCache.GetManagedLiveObjs()                         │\n│    - Filters by app's resource tracking labels                   │\n│    - Validates RBAC permissions                                  │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n           ↓\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│ 4. Reconcile (Match Target + Live)                               │\n│    - sync.Reconcile() [from gitops-engine]                       │\n│    - Creates ReconciliationResult with aligned lists             │\n│    - Deduplicates resources                                      │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n           ↓\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│ 5. Diff Calculation                                              │\n│    - argodiff.StateDiffs()                                       │\n│    - For each target/live pair:                                  │\n│      * Normalize both (remove fields Argo doesn't manage)        │\n│      * Compute diff (JSON, 3-way merge, or server-side)         │\n│    - Apply Ignore Differences config                             │\n│    - Result: DiffResultList with Modified flag per resource      │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n           ↓\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│ 6. Compute Sync Status                                           │\n│    - For each resource:                                          │\n│      * If diff.Modified OR target==nil OR live==nil             │\n│        └─> SyncStatusCodeOutOfSync                              │\n│      * Else                                                       │\n│        └─> SyncStatusCodeSynced                                  │\n│    - Overall: OutOfSync if ANY resource OutOfSync               │\n│    - Health: From liveStateCache health evaluation               │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n           ↓\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│ 7. Return comparisonResult                                       │\n│    ├─ syncStatus: SyncStatus (Synced/OutOfSync/Unknown)         │\n│    ├─ healthStatus: HealthStatus                                 │\n│    ├─ resources: []ResourceStatus                                │\n│    ├─ managedResources: For sync phase                          │\n│    └─ reconciliationResult: For sync execution                   │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n### 5. Diff Details\n\n**Location:** `/workspace/util/argo/diff/diff.go`\n\nThe diff system has multiple modes:\n\n```\nDiffConfig (Configurable)\n├─ Normalizers\n│  ├─ KnownTypes Normalizer (corev1_known_types.go)\n│  └─ Diff Normalizer (diff_normalizer.go)\n├─ IgnoreDifferences - paths to ignore\n├─ ResourceOverrides - system-level customization\n├─ TrackingMethod - label/annotation/both\n└─ ServerSideDiff - use kubectl server-side dry-run\n\nStateDiffs Algorithm:\n1. If serverSideDiff enabled:\n   └─> Use kubectl server-side dry-run to predict live after apply\n2. Else:\n   ├─> Apply 3-way merge (local/live/target)\n   ├─> Normalize live and predicted\n   ├─> Compare\n   └─> Return diff\n\nNormalization:\n- Removes Kubernetes internals (metadata.managedFields, etc.)\n- Ignores fields configured in ignoreDifferences\n- Applies resource overrides\n```\n\n### 6. Sync Operation Pipeline\n\n**Location:** `/workspace/controller/sync.go` (line 90)\n\nWhen `app.operation.sync` is set (user-initiated or auto-sync):\n\n```\nSyncAppState() Flow:\n\n┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│ 1. Initialize Sync                                        │\n│    - Get operation from operationState                    │\n│    - Determine if rollback or normal sync                 │\n│    - Set revision to sync to (or use request revision)    │\n└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n           ↓\n┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│ 2. Validate Sync Window                                   │\n│    - Check syncWindows in AppProject                      │\n│    - If blocked, return OperationRunning (retry later)   │\n└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n           ↓\n┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│ 3. Re-compare to Get Sync Targets                        │\n│    - Call CompareAppState with noRevisionCache=true      │\n│    - Ensures concrete revision SHA in syncResult         │\n│    - Return reconciliationResult (target manifest list)  │\n└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n           ↓\n┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│ 4. Prepare Sync Context                                  │\n│    - Get OpenAPI schema from cluster                     │\n│    - Get REST config (with impersonation if enabled)     │\n│    - Parse sync options (DryRun, Prune, Force, etc.)    │\n│    - Apply normalizations if RespectIgnoreDifferences    │\n└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n           ↓\n┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│ 5. Execute Sync via gitops-engine                        │\n│    sync.NewSyncContext()                                 │\n│      ├─ Options: Dry-run, Prune, Force, SSA, etc.       │\n│      └─ Resources Filter by project RBAC                 │\n│                                                           │\n│    syncCtx.Sync() (or Terminate() if terminating)       │\n│      ├─ Phase 1: Create/Replace resources                │\n│      ├─ Phase 2: Sync waves (parallel within wave)       │\n│      ├─ Phase 3: Prune resources if enabled              │\n│      ├─ Phase 4: Post-delete hooks                       │\n│      └─ Hook phases interspersed                         │\n│                                                           │\n│    GetState() returns:                                    │\n│      ├─ Phase: Succeeded/Failed/Error/Terminating        │\n│      ├─ Message: Status message                          │\n│      └─ Resources: []ResourceSyncResult per resource     │\n└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n           ↓\n┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│ 6. Update Operation State                                 │\n│    - Set phase, message, resources results               │\n│    - Update status.operationState                        │\n│    - For auto-sync: trigger app refresh                  │\n└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n### 7. State Machine Phases\n\n**OperationPhase values** (from gitops-engine):\n\n```\nPending       → Initial state, waiting to start\nRunning       → Sync in progress\nSuccess       → Completed successfully\nFailed        → Completed with failures\nError         → Operational error (config/permissions)\nTerminating   → User requested termination\nTerminated    → Termination completed\n```\n\n**ResourceSyncResult per resource:**\n\n```\nStatus: Synced / OutOfSync / Unknown / SyncFailed\nPhase: PreSync / Sync / PostSync / SyncFailed\nHookType: PreSync / PostSync (if applicable)\nHookPhase: Pending / Running / Success / Failed\nMessage: Human-readable result\n```\n\n### 8. Key Sync State Transitions\n\n```\nNormal Sync Flow (Healthy App):\n  OutOfSync → [user triggers sync] → OperationPending \n    → OperationRunning → OperationSucceeded \n    → Synced (after next refresh)\n\nAuto-Sync Flow:\n  OutOfSync → (app controller detects & auto-syncs)\n    → OperationPending → OperationRunning \n    → OperationSucceeded → Synced\n\nRetry Flow (Failed Sync):\n  OutOfSync → OperationRunning → OperationFailed \n    → (retry with backoff) → OperationRunning \n    → OperationSucceeded → Synced\n\nFailure States:\n  ComparisonError → status Unknown (can't determine state)\n  SyncError → OperationFailed (explicit failure)\n  InvalidSpec → OperationError (bad config)\n```\n\n### 11.
